20#include <stdint.h>

22/* To generate a Unicode 3.2 CNS11643.TXT, take
23 http://www.unicode.org/Public/Mappings/EASTASIA/OTHER/CNS11643.TXT
24 and add the following lines (see Unicode 3.2 UNIHAN.TXT):
25 0x12728 0x4EA0 # <CJK Ideograph>
26 0x1272F 0x51AB # <CJK Ideograph>
27 0x12734 0x52F9 # <CJK Ideograph>
28 */
29
30/* The following table contains quite some big hole but I'm not sure whether
31 it is a good idea to eliminate them. The algorithm gets slower (has to
32 use loops). [And I'm too lazy in the moment.]
33
34 The table can be generated using
35
36 egrep '^0x1' CNS11643.TXT |
37 awk '{print $1, $2}' | perl tab.pl
38
39 where tab.pl is:
40
41 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
42 $n=0;
43 while (<>) {
44 local($cns, $ucs4, %rest) = split;
45 local($u)=hex($ucs4);
46 local($c)=hex($cns)-0x12121;
47 printf ("\n ") if ($n % 4 eq 0);
48 ++$n;
49 printf (" [0x%04x] = 0x%04x,",
50 int($c / 256) * 94 + ($c & 0xff), $u);
51 }
52 printf ("\n");
53 ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
54*/
55const uint16_t __cns11643l1_to_ucs4_tab[] =

3659/* Glyphs for vertical variants. The table can be created using
3660

3662 awk '{ print $2, $1 }' | sort | egrep '^0xFE' | perl tab.pl

3665

3667 $n=0;

3669 local($ucs4, $cns, %rest) = split;
3670 local($u)=hex($ucs4);
3671 local($c)=hex($cns) - 0x10000;
3672 printf ("\n ") if ($n % 3 == 0);
3673 ++$n;
3674 printf (" [0x%04x] = \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",", $u - 0xfe30,
3675 $c < 0x100 ? $c : int($c/256), $c < 0x100 ? 0 : $c&255);
3676 }
3677 printf ("\n");
